*     05/04/85  11.24.03     BECx Hiz gPAfiKi - B CiCTEMY
      SUBROUTINE GETPEN(N)
C*
C******  BybOP  N-gO  pEPA  (N=1,2,...,6)
C*       HA gPAfOpOCTPOiTElE  WX4675
C*
      COMMON /PNUMB/ NPEN,NPOLD
      IF(N.GT.0.AND.N.LT.7) NPEN=N
      RETURN
      END
      SUBROUTINE PLOTBF(KX,KY,JOB)
C*
C******    g P A f O P  -  bYfEPizAciq
C*
C*    KOMAHdy BiPTYAlxHOgO gPAfplOTTEPA
C*    zApiCyBA`TCq B CiCTEMHyj fAjl ByBOdA
C*    B BidE pOClEdOBATElxHOCTi bAjTOB.
C*    dliHA pOClEdOBATElxHOCTi OpPEdElqETCq
C*    KOdOM KOMAHdy, YKAzAHHyM B 1-M bAjTE:
C*
C*    0 - pYCTAq KOMAHdA (OdHObAjTOBAq)
C*    1 - CMEHA bYMAgi HA plOTTEPE (1 bAjT)
C*    2 - YCTAHOBKA pEPA B HA~AlO  (1 bAjT)
C*    3 - CMEHA pEPA (HOMEP pEPA = 2-j bAjT)
C*    4 - dBivEHiE bEz PiCOBAHiq (5 bAjT) :
C*        bAjTy 2-3 : X-KOOPdiHATA (cElOE)
C*        bAjTy 4-5 : Y-KOOPdiHATA (cElOE)
C*    5 - dBivEHiE C PiCOBAHiEM (5 bAjT)
C*        AHAlOgi~HO KOMAHdE 4.
C*    6 - MAPKiPOBKA gPAfiKi (7 bAjT) :
C*        bAjTy 2-7 : iMq O~EPEdHOj pOPcii.
C*
      COMMON /SPLOT/ DX,DY
      DATA DX/0./, DY/0./
      COMMON /PLONAM/ NAME
      DATA NAME/'WX4675'/
      COMMON /PNUMB/ NPEN,NPOLD
      DATA NPEN/1/, NPOLD/1/
      COMMON /MARGRF/ MARK
      DATA MARK/1/
      DIMENSION MTEMP(4),MBUF(200)
      DATA LBUF/200/, NS/0/
      DATA NZER/0/
      EQUIVALENCE (KXNEW,MTEMP(2))
      EQUIVALENCE (KYNEW,MTEMP(4))
C
C---   HYvHA li MAPKiPOBKA :
C
      MSWOP=1
      IF(MARK.EQ.0B) GOTO 13
      LET=6
      DO 10 I=1,7
      ASSIGN 11 TO MBRET $ GOTO 100
  11  LET=IGETS(MARK,I-1)
  10  CONTINUE
      MARK=0B
C
C---    Y~ET CME}EHiq
C
  13  KXNEW = KX+INT(100.*DX)
      KYNEW = KY+INT(100.*DY)
C
C---    HE YCTAHOBKA li HA HA~AlO ?
C       pO KOHcY gPAfiKA dOCbPOCiM bYfEP
C       i CfOPMiPYEM HOByj MAPKEP
C
      IF(JOB.NE.0) GOTO 7
      LET=2 $ NZER=NZER+1 $ MSWOP=NZER.AND.1
      IF(MSWOP.EQ.0) MARK=1+NZER/2
      ASSIGN 99 TO MBRET $ GOTO 100
C
C---    HE CMEHA li bYMAgi
C
  7   IF(NAME.NE.'WXHOME') GOTO 1
      LET=1 $ NAME='WX4675'
      ASSIGN 1 TO MBRET $ GOTO 100
C
C---    HE HAdO li CMEHiTx pEPO
C
  1   IF(NPEN.EQ.NPOLD) GOTO 3
      NPOLD=NPEN $ LET=3
      ASSIGN 2 TO MBRET $ GOTO 100
  2   ASSIGN 3 TO MBRET $ LET=NPEN $ GOTO 100
C
C---    Oby~HOE dBivEHiE. CliB KOOPdiHAT
C
  3   LET=4 $ IF(JOB.GT.0) LET=5
      ASSIGN 4 TO MBRET $ GOTO 100
  4   MTEMP(1) = KXNEW.SHIFT.8
      MTEMP(3) = KYNEW.SHIFT.8
      DO 5 I=1,4
      LET=MTEMP(I) $ ASSIGN 5 TO MBRET
C
C---    zApiCx CiMBOlA B bYfEP
C
 100  CALL IPUTS(LET,MBUF,NS) $ NS=NS+1
      IF(NS.LT.6*LBUF.AND.MSWOP.NE.0) GOTO 102
      N1 = LOCF(MBUF) $ N2 = N1+LBUF-1
      N = (N1.SHIFT.-24).OR.(N2.AND.77777B).OR.0030 0000 0000 0000B
      N = JEXTRI(0,71B,N)
      DO 101 NS=1,LBUF
 101  MBUF(NS) = 0B
      NS = 0
 102  GOTO MBRET, (1,2,3,4,5,99)
C---
  5   CONTINUE
C---
  99  RETURN
      END
      SUBROUTINE PLOTC(KX,KY,JOB)
C*
C****      g P A f O P  -  C A L C O M P
C*
C*    KX,KY - KOOPdiHATy B {AgAX
C*            BiPTYAlxHOgO plOTTEPA
C*            Oby~HO {Ag = 0.01 MM.
C*    JOB   - KOd OpEPAcii :
C*       -1 : dBivEHiE C pOdHqTyM pEPOM
C*        1 : dBivEHiE C OpY}EHHyM pEPOM
C*        0 : YCTAHOBKA pEPA B HA~AlO
C*
C*    B ByzyBA`}Ej pPOgPAMME MOvET byTx
C*    OpiCAH  COMMON /SPLOT/ DX,DY
C*    zAdA`}ij CME}EHiE HA~AlA KOOPdiHAT
C*    B MilliMETPAX.
C*
      COMMON /SPLOT/ DX,DY
      COMMON /PLONAM/ NAME
      DATA NAME/'CALCOM'/, DX/0./, DY/0./
      DATA  XOLD/0./, YOLD/0./
C---
      X=0.01*KX+DX $ Y=0.01*KY+DY
      IF ( JOB ) 2,1,3
C---    YCTAHOBKA pEPA B HA~AlO
  1   CALL ENDGR
      GOTO 21
C---    bEz PiCOBAHiq
   2  CALL PENUP
      GOTO 20
C---    PiCOBAHiE
   3  CALL PENDWN
      R=SQRT((X-XOLD)**2+(Y-YOLD)**2)
      IF(R.LE.0.25) GOTO 20
      N=4*R
      DO 10 I=1,N
  10  CALL MOVEXY( (I*X+(N-I)*XOLD)/N, (I*Y+(N-I)*YOLD)/N )
C---
  20  CALL MOVEXY(X,Y)
  21  XOLD=X $ YOLD=Y
      RETURN
      END
      SUBROUTINE PLOTTX(KX,KY,JOB)
C*
C*****   g P A f O P  -  T E K T R O N I X
C*
      COMMON /SPLOT/ DX,DY
      COMMON /PLONAM/ NAME
      DIMENSION MBUF(20)
      DATA LB/114/, MFIR/0/
      DATA NAME/'TX4012'/, DX/0./, DY/0./
      DATA MBUF(1)/ 0722 0140 1004 0000B /
C---
C      "1" KX,KY  PABHA 0.01 MM
C      "1" DX,DY  PABHA 1.00 MM
C---
      JOB1=JOB
      KX1=100*DX+KX $ KY1=100*DY+KY
      IX=INT(0.0511*KX1) $ IY=INT(0.0511*KY1)
      IF(MFIR.NE.0) GOTO 1
      MFIR=1 $ NS=5
      J=JEXTRA( 1400 4000 0000 0000B, 61B, -1 )
C---
  1   IF(IX.LT.0) GOTO 11
      IF(IX.LT.1024) GOTO 2
      IX=1023 $ GOTO 12
  11  IX=0
  12  JOB1=-1
  2   IF(IY.LT.0) GOTO 13
      IF(IY.LT.780) GOTO 3
      IY=779 $ GOTO 14
  13  IY=0
  14  JOB1=-1
C---
  3   IF(JOB1.GT.0) GOTO 4
      CALL IPUTS(29,MBUF,NS)
      NS=NS+1
C---
  4   CALL IPUTS( IY.SHIFT.5.OR.40B, MBUF, NS )
      CALL IPUTS( IY.AND.37B.OR.140B,MBUF, NS+1)
      CALL IPUTS( IX.SHIFT.5.OR.40B, MBUF, NS+2)
      CALL IPUTS( IX.AND.37B.OR.100B,MBUF, NS+3)
      NS=NS+4
      IF(NS.LT.LB.AND.JOB.NE.0) RETURN
C---
      CALL IPUTS(0,MBUF,NS)
      J=LOCF(MBUF).AND.77777B.OR.1400 2000 3760 0000B
      J=JEXTRA(J,61B,-1)
      NS=0
      IF(JOB.EQ.0) MFIR=0
      RETURN
      END
      SUBROUTINE PLOTWX(KX,KY,JOB)
C*
C******   g P A f O P  -  W X 4 6 7 5
C*
      COMMON /SPLOT/ DX,DY
      COMMON /PLONAM/ NAME
      COMMON /PNUMB/ NPEN,NPOLD
      DATA NPEN/1/, NPOLD/1/
      DATA NAME/'WX4675'/,  DX/0./,  DY/0./
      DATA KGP/ 2243 0012 0000 0000B /
      DIMENSION STR(3),KOSTR(5)
      DATA KOSTR/'M','X-KOOR',',','Y-KOOR', 0240 0000 0000 0000B/
      DATA MER/0/, XOLD/0./, YOLD/0./
C----------------------------------
C       "1" KX,KY   PABHA 0.01 MM
C       "1" DX,DY   PABHA 1.00 MM
C       "1" WX4675  PABHA 0.10 MM
C----------------------------------
      IF(NAME.NE.'WXHOME') GOTO 2
      N=JOPER('CMEHi liCT HA PLOTTER',4,1)
      NAME='WX4675'
  2   IF(NPEN.EQ.NPOLD) GOTO 3
      NPOLD=NPEN
      KOSTR=NPEN.SHIFT.-32.OR.KGP
      N=LOCF(KOSTR).AND.77777B.OR.140 0000B
      N=JEXTRA(N,61B,77777B)
  3   X=0.1*KX+10*DX $ Y=0.1*KY+10*DY
      N=0
      IF(X.EQ.XOLD .AND. Y.EQ.YOLD) RETURN
      IF(JOB.LE.0) KOSTR='M'
      IF(JOB.GT.0.AND.MER.EQ.0) KOSTR='D'
      CALL PUTG(KOSTR(2),X,1,4,0,IPOZ)
      CALL PUTG(KOSTR(4),Y,1,4,0,IPOZ)
      IF(X.LT.0. .OR. X.GT.3450.) GOTO 200
      IF(Y.LT.0. .OR. Y.GT.2600.) GOTO 200
      DO 1 I=1,26
      LET=IGETS(KOSTR,I-1)
      IF(LET.EQ.32) GOTO 1
      CALL IPUTS(LET,STR,N)
      N=N+1
   1  CONTINUE
      MER=0
      N=LOCF(STR).AND.77777B.OR.0740 0000B
      N=JEXTRA(N,61B,77777B)
      I=N.AND.4.OR.0
      IF(I.EQ.0) GOTO 10
      GOTO 100
 200  MER=1
      IF(JOB.EQ.0) GOTO 10
C---    PRINT ByPEzAH iz |KOHOMii
 100    CONTINUE
  10  XOLD=X $ YOLD=Y
      RETURN
      END

 A/ARRD/K:,NAME,       ALGOL/ INTERPRETIERENDE ROUTINE    3.1.74
C  ROUTINEN FUER FELDVEREINBARUNGEN
C  A/ARRD/K: ADRESSBUCH SCHON SKALAR ALLOKIERT
C  A/ARRD/V: ADRESSBUCH NOCH NICHT ALLOKIERT
C  PARAMETER:  MAGAZIN: FELDGRENZEN
C              I11: ANZAHL DER GRENZENPAARE
C              I12: ANZAHL DER FELDER
C              I13: SKALARE FELDADRESSE
C              I14: RK-ADRESSE
C
 C:,BSS,
 SYSBACK*:,SUBP,.
 AUG:,EQU,             21B
 D:,EQU,               22B
 I15G:,EQU,            23B
 A:,EQU,               23B                AB I=1
 B:,EQU,               31B
 L:,EQU,               40B
 K:,EQU,               12
 N:,EQU,               11
 I:,EQU,               10
 FW:,EQU,              13
 A/ARRD/K:,NTR,        3
 9,VTM,                C
 15,XTS,               -1                 BN
 15,A-X,               -2                 AN
 9,A+X,                =I1-C
 ,UJ,                  *+2
 A/ARRD/V:,ENTRY,
 ,NTR,                 3
 ,XTS,
 :9,VTM,               C
 ,STX,                 AUG
 N,MTJ,                I
 BOUNDS:I,STX,         B
 I,STX,                A
 I,UTM,                -1
 I,V1M,                BOUNDS
 15,ATX,
 NEXTARR:N,MTJ,        I
 N,XTA,                B
 N,A-X,                A
 ,U1A,                 BD/ERR
 9,A+X,                =I1-C
 ,ATX,                 D

C** FPACK-BCDREAD*(FT,LUN)
C                  BENUTZERROUTINE ZUR EROEFFNUNG EINER FORMAT-
C                  GESTEUERTEN EINGABE
